#include <math.h>
        int main(void) {

        /* With some toolchains (MSYS2/mingw for example) the compiler
         * provides various builtins which are not really implemented and
         * fall back to the stdlib where they aren't provided and fail at
         * build/link time. In case the user provides a header, including
         * the header didn't lead to the function being defined, and the
         * function we are checking isn't a builtin itself we assume the
         * builtin is not functional and we just error out. */
        #if !0 && !defined(isfinite) && !0
            #error "No definition for __builtin_isfinite found in the prefix"
        #endif

        #ifdef __has_builtin
            #if !__has_builtin(__builtin_isfinite)
                #error "__builtin_isfinite not found"
            #endif
        #elif ! defined(isfinite)
            __builtin_isfinite;
        #endif
        return 0;
        }
-----------

#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

#define repcmp(z) (memcmp((const char *)&foo.x, z, sizeof(foo.x)) == 0)

const struct {
  char before[16];
  long double x;
  char after[8];
} foo = {{'\0'}, -123456789.0, {'\0'}};

int main(void) {
  switch (sizeof(foo.x)) {
  case 8: {
    if (repcmp(
            ((const char[]){0000, 0000, 0000, 0124, 0064, 0157, 0235, 0301}))) {
      fprintf(stdout, "IEEE_DOUBLE_LE");
      return 0;
    }
    if (repcmp(
            ((const char[]){0301, 0235, 0157, 0064, 0124, 0000, 0000, 0000}))) {
      fprintf(stdout, "IEEE_DOUBLE_BE");
      return 0;
    }
    fprintf(stdout, "UNKNOWN");
    return 1;
  }
  case 12: {
    if (repcmp(((const char[]){0000, 0000, 0000, 0000, 0240, 0242, 0171, 0353,
                               0031, 0300, 0000, 0000}))) {
      fprintf(stdout, "INTEL_EXTENDED_12_BYTES_LE");
      return 0;
    }
    if (repcmp(((const char[]){0300, 0031, 0000, 0000, 0353, 0171, 0242, 0240,
                               0000, 0000, 0000, 0000}))) {
      fprintf(stdout, "MOTOROLA_EXTENDED_12_BYTES_BE");
      return 0;
    }
    fprintf(stdout, "UNKNOWN");
    return 1;
  }
  case 16: {
    if (repcmp(
            ((const char[]){0000, 0000, 0000, 0000, 0240, 0242, 0171, 0353,
                            0031, 0300, 0000, 0000, 0000, 0000, 0000, 0000}))) {
      fprintf(stdout, "INTEL_EXTENDED_16_BYTES_LE");
      return 0;
    }
    if (repcmp(
            ((const char[]){0300, 0031, 0326, 0363, 0105, 0100, 0000, 0000,
                            0000, 0000, 0000, 0000, 0000, 0000, 0000, 0000}))) {
      fprintf(stdout, "IEEE_QUAD_BE");
      return 0;
    }
    if (repcmp(
            ((const char[]){0000, 0000, 0000, 0000, 0000, 0000, 0000, 0000,
                            0000, 0000, 0100, 0105, 0363, 0326, 0031, 0300}))) {
      fprintf(stdout, "IEEE_QUAD_LE");
      return 0;
    }
    if (repcmp(
            ((const char[]){0000, 0000, 0000, 0124, 0064, 0157, 0235, 0301,
                            0000, 0000, 0000, 0000, 0000, 0000, 0000, 0000}))) {
      fprintf(stdout, "IBM_DOUBLE_DOUBLE_LE");
      return 0;
    }
    if (repcmp(
            ((const char[]){0301, 0235, 0157, 0064, 0124, 0000, 0000, 0000,
                            0000, 0000, 0000, 0000, 0000, 0000, 0000, 0000}))) {
      fprintf(stdout, "IBM_DOUBLE_DOUBLE_BE");
      return 0;
    }
    fprintf(stdout, "UNKNOWN");
    return 1;
  }
  }
}

    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m        The first form should be preferred.[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m    bins : sequence or int, optional[39;49;00m
    [33m        The bin specification:[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m        * A sequence of arrays describing the monotonically increasing bin[39;49;00m
    [33m          edges along each dimension.[39;49;00m
    [33m        * The number of bins for each dimension (nx, ny, ... =bins)[39;49;00m
    [33m        * The number of bins for all dimensions (nx=ny=...=bins).[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m    range : sequence, optional[39;49;00m
    [33m        A sequence of length D, each an optional (lower, upper) tuple giving[39;49;00m
    [33m        the outer bin edges to be used if the edges are not given explicitly in[39;49;00m
    [33m        `bins`.[39;49;00m
    [33m        An entry of None in the sequence results in the minimum and maximum[39;49;00m
    [33m        values being used for the corresponding dimension.[39;49;00m
    [33m        The default, None, is equivalent to passing a tuple of D None values.[39;49;00m
    [33m    density : bool, optional[39;49;00m
    [33m        If False, the default, returns the number of samples in each bin.[39;49;00m
    [33m        If True, returns the probability *density* function at the bin,[39;49;00m
    [33m        ``bin_count / sample_count / bin_volume``.[39;49;00m
    [33m    weights : (N,) array_like, optional[39;49;00m
    [33m        An array of values `w_i` weighing each sample `(x_i, y_i, z_i, ...)`.[39;49;00m
    [33m        Weights are normalized to 1 if density is True. If density is False,[39;49;00m
    [33m        the values of the returned histogram are equal to the sum of the[39;49;00m
    [33m        weights belonging to the samples falling into each bin.[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m    Returns[39;49;00m
    [33m    -------[39;49;00m
    [33m    H : ndarray[39;49;00m
    [33m        The multidimensional histogram of sample x. See density and weights[39;49;00m
    [33m        for the different possible semantics.[39;49;00m
    [33m    edges : tuple of ndarrays[39;49;00m
    [33m        A tuple of D arrays describing the bin edges for each dimension.[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m    See Also[39;49;00m
    [33m    --------[39;49;00m
    [33m    histogram: 1-D histogram[39;49;00m
    [33m    histogram2d: 2-D histogram[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m    Examples[39;49;00m

    [33m    ----------[39;49;00m
    [33m    fname : filename, file handle or pathlib.Path[39;49;00m
    [33m        If the filename ends in ``.gz``, the file is automatically saved in[39;49;00m
    [33m        compressed gzip format.  `loadtxt` understands gzipped files[39;49;00m
    [33m        transparently.[39;49;00m
    [33m    X : 1D or 2D array_like[39;49;00m
    [33m        Data to be saved to a text file.[39;49;00m
    [33m    fmt : str or sequence of strs, optional[39;49;00m
    [33m        A single format (%10.5f), a sequence of formats, or a[39;49;00m
    [33m        multi-format string, e.g. 'Iteration %d -- %10.5f', in which[39;49;00m
    [33m        case `delimiter` is ignored. For complex `X`, the legal options[39;49;00m
    [33m        for `fmt` are:[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m        * a single specifier, ``fmt='%.4e'``, resulting in numbers formatted[39;49;00m
    [33m          like ``' (%s+%sj)' % (fmt, fmt)``[39;49;00m
    [33m        * a full string specifying every real and imaginary part, e.g.[39;49;00m
    [33m          ``' %.4e %+.4ej %.4e %+.4ej %.4e %+.4ej'`` for 3 columns[39;49;00m

    [33m          and imaginary part must have separate specifiers,[39;49;00m

    [33m    comments : str, optional[39;49;00m

    [33m        to mark them as comments. Default: '# ',  as expected by e.g.[39;49;00m

    [33m    Notes[39;49;00m
    [33m    -----[39;49;00m
    [33m    Further explanation of the `fmt` parameter[39;49;00m
    [33m    (``%[flag]width[.precision]specifier``):[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m    flags:[39;49;00m
    [33m        ``-`` : left justify[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m        ``+`` : Forces to precede result with + or -.[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m        ``0`` : Left pad the number with zeros instead of space (see width).[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m    width:[39;49;00m
    [33m        Minimum number of characters to be printed. The value is not truncated[39;49;00m
    [33m        if it has more characters.[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m    precision:[39;49;00m
    [33m        - For integer specifiers (eg. ``d,i,o,x``), the minimum number of[39;49;00m
    [33m          digits.[39;49;00m
    [33m        - For ``e, E`` and ``f`` specifiers, the number of digits to print[39;49;00m
    [33m          after the decimal point.[39;49;00m
    [33m        - For ``g`` and ``G``, the maximum number of significant digits.[39;49;00m
    [33m        - For ``s``, the maximum number of characters.[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m    specifiers:[39;49;00m
    [33m        ``c`` : character[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m        ``d`` or ``i`` : signed decimal integer[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m        ``e`` or ``E`` : scientific notation with ``e`` or ``E``.[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m        ``f`` : decimal floating point[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m        ``g,G`` : use the shorter of ``e,E`` or ``f``[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m        ``o`` : signed octal[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m        ``s`` : string of characters[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m        ``u`` : unsigned decimal integer[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m        ``x,X`` : unsigned hexadecimal integer[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m    This explanation of ``fmt`` is not complete, for an exhaustive[39;49;00m

    [33m    References[39;49;00m

    [33m        case `delimiter` is ignored. For complex `X`, the legal options[39;49;00m

    [33m[39;49;00m

    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m    flags:[39;49;00m

    [33m          digits.[39;49;00m

    [33m          after the decimal point.[39;49;00m

    [33m    specifiers:[39;49;00m

    [33m[39;49;00m

    [33m[39;49;00m

    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m        ``f`` : decimal floating point[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m

    [33m        ``o`` : signed octal[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m        ``s`` : string of characters[39;49;00m

    [33m        multi-format string, e.g. 'Iteration %d -- %10.5f', in which[39;49;00m
    [33m        case `delimiter` is ignored. For complex `X`, the legal options[39;49;00m
    [33m        for `fmt` are:[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m

    [33m        * a full string specifying every real and imaginary part, e.g.[39;49;00m

    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m    flags:[39;49;00m

    [33m          digits.[39;49;00m

    [33m          after the decimal point.[39;49;00m
    [33m        - For ``g`` and ``G``, the maximum number of significant digits.[39;49;00m

    [33m    specifiers:[39;49;00m

    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m        ``d`` or ``i`` : signed decimal integer[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m        ``e`` or ``E`` : scientific notation with ``e`` or ``E``.[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m        ``f`` : decimal floating point[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m        ``g,G`` : use the shorter of ``e,E`` or ``f``[39;49;00m

    [33m        ``o`` : signed octal[39;49;00m
    [33m[39;49;00m
    [33m        ``s`` : string of characters[39;49;00m

    [33m        ``u`` : unsigned decimal integer[39;49;00m
